He Jian Returns to Changsha from Hengzhou

Farewell Dinner for He Yingqin on the Evening of the 6th

Changsha Correspondence: The military affairs of Hunan Province have come to an end. Yesterday, on the 5th, Liu Wendao came to Hunan by plane on the North Persian, representing General Commander Chiang to express his condolences to He Yingqin and He Jian and to discuss all the aftermath. Liu brought a letter from Chiang to He Jian, which said, "Brother Yunqiao, I salute you. In this campaign against the rebels, your department sacrificed everything to be loyal to the Party and the country, and your achievements are great. It adds glory to the history of the revolution. Zhongzheng is also honored. Brother Chensu came here and learned about the situation at that time. I am especially grateful. I hope that you will lead your troops to destroy this chief before you eat, so as to secure the Party and the country. I have specially asked Brother Chen to come to discuss everything in person and to express my condolences. Sincerely, Chiang Kai-shek, July 4th, 5:00." At that time, He Jian was still directing the various departments in Hengzhou. Upon hearing that Liu Wendao had come to Hunan as a representative of General Commander Chiang and that He Yingqin had to return to Wuhan, he took two cars from Hengzhou back to the province at 6:10 pm on the 6th. He arrived at the Xiaowumen train station in Changsha at 5:40 pm, where more than 100 people from the Party, government, and military circles welcomed him at the station. He immediately boarded a chartered car and went straight to the large living room of the provincial government, where he had light refreshments with the welcoming people and reported on the situation at the front. Those who returned to the province with He included only Secretary-General Liu Pengnian and Wen Susong, a senior staff officer of the Wuhan Headquarters. That evening, He prepared a Western dinner in the large flower hall of the provincial government to entertain He Yingqin and all the staff of the headquarters to show his farewell. Figures from the Party, government, and military circles accompanied the dinner, and the only foreign guests were Liu Wendao, Zhang Buxian, the representative of Guizhou Province, Huang Xingyi, the representative of Jiangxi Province, and several pilots. During the dinner, He Jian reported on the course of the battle. Then, He Yingqin gave a speech, generally stating that the greatest reason for achieving a great victory in the shortest possible time was that all the generals and soldiers were able to follow the plan set by the headquarters and work together to implement it, and secondly, that all the troops had a spirit of hard work and sacrifice, and thirdly, that the weather was very good and our aircraft were able to achieve great results and inflict heavy losses on the enemy. Finally, he reported on the situation of the battles on the Jinpu, Longhai, and Pinghan lines, and that Yan and Feng would be annihilated sooner or later. However, the current focus should be on the disturbances caused by the communists in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, which is not a simple military problem. He hoped that the Party, government, and military would unite and share the responsibility of finding ways to eliminate them so that the people could look forward to peace and alleviate the hidden worries of the Party and the country. Liu Wendao then gave a speech reporting on the situation he had observed on the Longhai and Pinghan fronts recently. Then, they toasted each other until 10:30 pm before they dispersed.

Competition Between Hantieh and Northeast Railway

Shenyang Correspondence: The South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu) system has always used the gold standard. All passenger and freight fares are officially collected in gold certificates. In the midst of rising gold prices and falling silver prices, they still maintain their old position without any changes, intending to take advantage of the situation and seize profits for themselves. However, this was discerned by our Northeast transportation authorities, who specially implemented price reductions and combined transportation on state-owned railways, reducing freight rates to 50% and reducing customs duties to 30%. For those going to Goubangzi, customs duties are completely waived. In terms of passenger tickets, those who hold reclamation farmer certificates are only charged 30% of the price, and ordinary passenger tickets that hold three-line intermodal transport tickets are also reduced by 20% to 30%. The above are all based on national currency, and two yuan of national currency is equivalent to one gold certificate. Due to the low freight rates of state-owned railways, which are very different from Mantetsu, domestic merchants have shifted their transportation trends. Mantetsu has been greatly impacted and its revenue has fallen sharply. However, the Japanese did not reflect on themselves and reduce freight rates to plan for the future of Mantetsu. They only blamed our transportation for not reducing transportation prices. This is truly unreasonable. Recently, the Japanese merchants in Sipingjie, an extraterritorial area only a short distance from Shenyang, witnessed that various commercial groups in the special zone transported products to Yingkou, Tianjin, and Guannei through the national road, with three or four cars being shipped out every day. Mantetsu, on the contrary, regarded this as a very serious problem and held a citizens' assembly for three days to study countermeasures against the competition of the Chinese railway and ways to save it. The first issue was the 50% reduction in freight rates on the Datong line. The final strategy was to arouse the popular propaganda of the entire Japanese opinion circle so that all the Japanese people would pay attention and enable the leaders of the Mantetsu headquarters to save it. Whether it can be effective depends on how it is implemented. Now, the comparison between the freight prices of each car on the state-owned railway three-line intermodal transport and Mantetsu shows that the difference is huge as follows: (1) The freight for one car of soybeans starting from Sipingjie Station, passing through the four Tao, Datong, Beining, and three lines connected by intermodal transport to Yingkou is 377.15 yuan in national currency. (2) The freight for one car of soybeans starting from Sipingjie Station directly from the Mantetsu line to Yingkou is 293.7 yuan in gold certificates, which should be converted to 564.8 yuan in silver dollars at a 52% discount. Therefore, it can save 188.65 silver dollars per car to reach Yingkou via the state-owned three-line road. Therefore, the Chinese people abandoned Mantetsu like discarding it, and there was not a single car loaded. Not only did the freight from Sipingjie to Yingkou decrease, but also the passenger tickets for passengers from Heilongjiang Province and west of Zhengjiatun who passed through Tianjin and Yingkou were all going down west. Therefore, the Japanese studied the reduction of fares on the Datong line by 50% to counter our state-owned railway. However, alleviating the economic suffering of some people, we do not hate the speculation of the Japanese and hope that they can realize it as soon as possible. (7th)

Zhang Xueliang Inspects the Naval Fleet

Shenyang Correspondence: According to people from Huludao on the 5th, it rained heavily all night on the 3rd. Zhang Xueliang stayed on the island in the fourth floor of the railway club. On the morning of the 4th, the rain cleared. At 3:00 pm, Zhang, accompanied by Hu Ruoyu, Zhu Guangmu, Gao Jiyi, Yang Zhengzhi, and more than ten attendants, inspected the Northeast Navy fleets on the Hongji ship, accompanied by Shen Honglie. When Zhang arrived at the ship, all the ships raised flags and fired 17 salutes. The entire fleet performed the welcome ceremony on the ship. Shen Honglie and Ling Xiao, commander of the First Fleet, led Zhang into the commander's office for a short rest. All officers above the rank of deputy captain and chief engineer were promoted in turn. After the officials withdrew, they began to review the various forms. Next was the inspection of personnel and internal affairs. Then, they watched the joint fleet exercise on the deck of the Haiqi ship. The fleet exercise assumed that the Haiqi and Haishen ships were the A army, commanded by Ling Xiao, the captain of the Haiqi ship, and the Yongxiang and Chuyu ships were the B army, commanded by Liu Tianfu, the captain of the Zhenhai ship. All the soldiers cooperated, and the situation was very tense. For a time, the sound of cannons, the sound of orders, and the sound of military reports were heard, and planes circled in the sky and fired downwards and dropped bombs. The bombs fell into the water and emitted black smoke, which disappeared after two minutes. Gong Runxing, the deputy team leader of the Haiqi ship, who sank the Russian flagship in the Battle of Jiang, also participated in the exercise. The two sides fought fiercely until 5:40 pm before they stopped. Zhang praised all the soldiers. At 6:00 pm, Zhang had not yet left the ship to land. According to reports, the Haiqi ship is the largest cruiser in China, more than 420 feet long, with more than 20 large and small cannons and 5 torpedo cannons. More than 1,200 soldiers also participated in the actual exercise. Zhang is still on the island. It is rumored that Mr. Zhang went to Beidaihe for summer vacation after inspecting the navy on the afternoon of the 4th, but that statement is not accurate. (6th)

Record of the Huludao Port Opening Ceremony (Continued)

It was heard that the Port Authority was planning to visit the head of the office, Ning Mengyan, at the No. 1 office building on the seaside to discuss matters. Upon arriving at the No. 1 office building, it was discovered that it was the Dutch port management company. When asked about the Port Authority, the Chinese staff replied that it was at the No. 4 office building in Dongshan, already far away in the deep mountains. As the sun was setting, there would be no way to proceed if refused. Therefore, it was thought that the Naval Police School was closer to the No. 1 building, so a change of plan was made to go there. The principal, Wu Lixian, and the Dean of Education, Yang Changhou, were met, and they kindly agreed to arrange accommodation. According to Mr. Wu, the Naval Police School had been established for five years and was the first naval education institution in the Northeast. The first class of navigation and the second class of marine engineering had both graduated and been assigned to various coastal and river defense ships for training and service. The third class was also a navigation class and would not graduate until next year. This year, due to the Navy Department's order for the Bohai Fleet to take charge of Qingdao's coastal defense, the Naval Police students were transferred to Qingdao to study. Currently, the school only had a few dozen recruits left. Naval work was inherently difficult, and promotions were more difficult than in the army, but the pay was better. Sailors had to undergo four years of training before being promoted to Petty Officer Third Class, and being promoted to Sergeant First Class was already not easy. Although there were special merits that could lead to promotion to Lieutenant, such cases were rare. If there were vacancies for officers on the ships, they should be filled by the most outstanding students in service and academics. The school's annual expenses were about 140,000 to 150,000 yuan. The school site was borrowed from the Port Authority, and now, due to the urgent need for construction, it had to be relocated. Commander Shen planned to build a new school building in Dongshan, but the plans were still in progress. The Northeast naval system was divided into coastal defense and river defense groups. Zhang Xueliang concurrently served as the Commander-in-Chief of the Bohai Fleet, and Shen Honglie was the Deputy Commander-in-Chief. There were a total of seven warships: Haiqi, Haichen, Zhaohao, Tongan, Zhenhai, Yongxiang, and Chuyu, with Haiqi being the largest, serving as an aircraft carrier. These seven warships were not enough to fulfill the responsibility of consolidating national defense, and there was an urgent need to add new ships. However, the Northeast's financial resources were insufficient, and with the rising price of gold, the current price of building ships was about 7,000 to 8,000 yuan per ton. Building a 10,000-ton warship would cost no less than 10 million yuan. The Northeast Navy's annual expenditure was more than 3 million yuan, which was not a small amount, but it was still far less than the Northeast Army's annual expenditure. Commander Shen, because Commander-in-Chief Zhang was attending the opening ceremony, led the Haiqi and other five ships from Qingdao to the island the day before. Tonight, there would be a banquet for Zhang at the school, after which he would board the Haichen warship because Zhang was going to observe naval anti-aircraft exercises tomorrow morning. Originally, it was scheduled to guide the guests to visit the warships immediately after the opening ceremony today, but the wind and waves were too strong, and it was quite dangerous to carry people in sampans, so it was canceled. Tomorrow's anti-aircraft plan was that Zhang would board the Haiqi warship at 5:00 AM, and Shen would order the Haichen to sail out of the port as an enemy warship. At this time, Zhang would inspect the Haiqi's internal affairs and the officers' and soldiers' duties. After 6:00 AM, the Haiqi dispatched two seaplanes, one for reconnaissance and one for bombing. More than ten minutes later, the reconnaissance plane returned to the ship and reported that an enemy warship was found more than ten nautical miles away. Upon receiving the report, the Haiqi immediately engaged the enemy. After the two sides approached, they began anti-aircraft exercises. Bombers soared over the enemy warship and dropped bombs. Reconnaissance planes frequently reported the enemy warship's movements to the home ship. At 11:00 AM, the enemy warship retreated, and the Haiqi returned to port in formation. The exercise was then completed. It was heard that Zhang was scheduled to visit Beidaihe on the fourth and then return to Liaoning.

After sunset, the Haiqi and other five ships emitted searchlights to inspect the entire island. The Naval Police School frequently used light signals to report that the island was safe. The station's lights were as bright as a picture. From the club to the foot of the mountain, several gasoline lamps were added. There was no power plant on the island yet. The station's lights were temporarily prepared by the railway bureau. The generator transported by the port management company had not yet been installed. At this time, taking off my coat to face the wind, the weather felt like late autumn. Listening quietly to the sound of the pines like rain and the chirping of insects like singing, the rushing sound of the waves and the barking of village dogs were also carried by the wind. Looking up at the crescent moon and the twinkling stars, one suddenly felt like transcending the world. Suddenly, a soldier shouted a password, which made one shudder. After 10:00 PM, the searchlights of the ships stopped, and the four large characters "Opening Ceremony Commemoration" formed by electric torches were displayed. Principal Wu, because it was late, sent Assistant Instructor Tao to guide me to rest at Captain Liu's residence.

On the third day, I woke up in the dim morning light. The rising sun had just appeared on the horizon, its color as red as a fireball. The sea water, reflecting it, shot out rays of light. The myriad green mountains seen yesterday were now shrouded in white clouds. The morning breeze felt refreshing. I toured the entire island to visit everything. Since the start of construction, the island had been showing a vibrant scene. More than 3,000 workers were engaged in the work of blasting mountains and filling the sea. There were more than a dozen earthen houses north of the station, all newly built, selling food, but there were no hotels yet. The post office and telegraph office had only been open for two days, and the stationmaster was still working on the train. There were three radio stations, two shortwave and one longwave, all under the jurisdiction of the Northeast Transportation Committee. The island's passenger train ran four times a day in each direction. The island's telephone was also temporarily installed by the port management company to facilitate office work. Most of the guests attending the ceremony were from the silver and business sectors, followed by the industrial sector. Most of these people wanted to take the opportunity of the ceremony to assess the situation and plan to buy land in preparation for future business operations. Upon arriving at the island, they realized that the 30 li of land had already been bought by the Port Authority. Now, it was only for rent, not for sale. The regulations for temporary land rental stipulated that the monthly rent was six yuan per mu for first-class land, five yuan per mu for second-class land, and four yuan per mu for third-class land. If the island's commercial market did not develop, that would be fine, but if it did, the land price would be monopolized by the Port Authority. Therefore, some people had already created an atmosphere, claiming that Huludao was not suitable for building commercial shops and should only be developed as a residential area, and that a commercial area should be developed in Lianshan. There were no bedbugs or mosquitoes on the island, but there were too many flies. The outer layer of each mountain was yellow sandy soil two or three feet thick, and inside was stone, so only green grass was seen, and there were no shady trees. There were some old trees that were leaning and slanting, no more than ten feet tall, which was the biggest shortcoming in terms of scenery. A few days ago, when the port management company was excavating Banlashan by the sea, a thousand-foot cliff was cut, overlooking the sea. Seven workers climbed bravely, but suddenly encountered a rock collapse, resulting in two deaths and five injuries. This was the third opening of the port. The first time, the injured had been admitted to the temporary hospital for treatment, and the dead had been buried. It was not known how the compensation would be handled, and there had been no news yet. There was also a major drinking water problem on the island that urgently needed to be solved, because the sea water was salty and bitter, and even after being filtered by sand, it was still unclean. Wells had recently been dug, but they only maintained the current situation. If the port developed in the future and the population increased to hundreds of thousands, there would be no way to solve the problem. Currently, the port management company planned to build natural reservoirs on the mountain tops, but this method had to go through three to five years of testing the natural rainfall before the drinking water supply standard could be determined. They were also afraid that this method would fail, so they also asked well-digging experts to survey the underground water sources in order to dig large wells. Ning Wu, courtesy name Mengyan, the head of the Huludao Port Authority, was the Chief Adjutant of the Northeast Border Defense Army Commander-in-Chief's Office and was very close to Gao Jiyi, the Director of the Beining Railway Bureau. According to Mr. Ning, the main tasks of port construction were breakwaters, wharves, and sea walls. The breakwater was 7,600 feet long, the wharf was 4,600 feet long, and the sea wall was 2,360 feet long. The water depth at the wharf was 30 to 33 feet, which could accommodate ships of more than 50,000 tons. Currently, ordinary merchant ships were only 5,000 to 6,000 tons, with the largest being 12,000 tons. However, the Suez and Panama canals were only 27 feet deep, and large Western merchant ships were restricted by the two canals and could not come east. Therefore, the port's water depth of 33 feet was sufficient. The port area with a depth of 30 feet or more was 8 million square feet, which could accommodate 13 merchant ships of more than 5,000 tons at the same time and load 1.5 million tons of cargo per year. The first phase of port construction was leveling mountains and filling the sea, from May 1st to the end of June, which was the preparation period for the project. July 1st was the official start of work. The port management company had prepared cranes, rock drills, dredgers, locomotives, ships, dormitories, offices, factories, and hospitals and had made some progress. The earth-filling project had completed 60,000 cubic yards, and the wharf had completed more than 90 feet. Currently, they were blasting the rocks of Gaoliangduo Mountain and Banlashan. The first phase of the project was expected to take about one year. The second phase of construction was the wharf. The land-based construction, such as stations, railways, warehouses, and municipal planning, was all handled by the port staff, who were currently surveying and drawing. As soon as the drawings were completed, they would start planning and construction in sequence. The reporter, having completed his task, took a train to Lianshan on the same day and transferred to train No. 102 at 6:00 PM to enter the pass. He arrived in Tianjin at 7:00 AM on the fourth and recorded this to comfort the readers. (July 4th)

Han Merchants Procure Sichuan Rice to Relieve Famine

Hankou Correspondence: Recently, rice prices here have soared, greatly affecting the people's food supply. Rice merchants in Hankou are willing to raise funds themselves to procure rice from Wanxian, Chongqing, and other places in Sichuan, transport it to Hankou, and sell it at a fair price. They have submitted a request to the Hankou General Chamber of Commerce to notify General Liu in Chongqing, Commander Wang in Wanxian, and the two chambers of commerce in Chongqing and Wanxian to issue permits for transportation to avoid difficulties along the way. The Hankou Chamber of Commerce, upon receiving the request, praised the merchants for raising funds to procure Sichuan rice to relieve the famine and specifically notified the Sichuan side with a letter that read, "We are writing to inform you that we have recently received a stamped request from rice merchants in Hankou, including Yu Maoqian, Xin Tai, and Xie Changxiang, stating that the source of rice is scarce, the price is rising, and the people are having difficulty obtaining food. They request permission to procure Sichuan rice, transport it to Hankou, and sell it at a fair price to help the people's livelihood. We have learned that Wuhan's rice supply has always been sourced from Hunan and Jiangxi, but the source has been interrupted, and the price has suddenly risen, causing great difficulty for the people's food supply. The merchants, in view of this, are willing to raise funds themselves to procure 5,000 shi of Sichuan rice from Wanxian and Chongqing, transport it to Hankou, and sell it at a fair price. They fear that the truth may not be clear in the area, causing obstruction. Therefore, they request that the Chamber of Commerce issue a letter to notify the two chambers of commerce in Wanxian and Chongqing, as well as General Liu, Commander of the 21st Army in Chongqing, and Commander Wang of the Wanxian Command, to allow transportation and issue passports to avoid difficulties along the way and help the people's livelihood and maintain the people's food supply, which is a public good. The Wuhan people's food supply is already showing signs of famine, and the merchants' plan to raise funds to procure Sichuan rice is a matter of urgency. In addition to issuing separate letters, we are writing to request that you investigate and provide passports if the merchants come to Sichuan to procure rice to ensure and alleviate the neighboring famine. We would be grateful." The Hankou General Chamber of Commerce, in order to relieve the rice famine and suppress the price of rice, had resolved to procure 1,000 shi of Xiaojiao rice from Shanghai and sell it at a fair price in Hankou. It has been implemented since the sixth, and about 1,000 bags have been sold in the past three days. The two directors, Wang Linfu and Li Dezhai, personally supervised everything. The price was 760 yuan per sheng, which was less than 16 yuan per shi. For those who bought whole shi, it was 16 yuan and 5 jiao. According to the cost in Shanghai, each shi was losing more than one yuan. The rice was about the same quality as the third-grade rice from machine rice mills. The fair price sale was from 6:00 AM to 11:00 AM. It was heard that 2,500 bags of rice had arrived, and at least 10,000 bags were still to come. If the price could not be stabilized, procurement would have to continue.

Wuhu Express Letter

This morning at 9:00 AM, people from all walks of life held a memorial meeting for the fourth anniversary of the Northern Expedition of the 79th Revolutionary Army at the Song and Dance Theater on Zhongshan Road. More than 200 representatives attended. The chairman of the Municipal Party Committee reported on the Revolutionary Army's suppression of reactionaries and completion of the National Revolution, as well as the process of launching the Northern Expedition. He also said that the Revolutionary Army was still continuing to eliminate counter-revolutionary work and hoped that the people would unanimously support it. All organs and groups stopped working, and all stores in the city closed for one day to celebrate, as announced by the General Chamber of Commerce.

The Anhui Finance Commissioner's Office of the Ministry of Finance recently stated that the remittance of funds from various likin bureaus was too delayed, and it would be difficult to improve tax revenue without fundamental rectification. It was decided to convene a meeting of likin bureau chiefs on the 21st of this month. Yesterday, telegrams had been sent to the 37 likin bureau chiefs in Anhui, instructing them to attend the meeting in Wuhu on time and without delay.

Sun Gongming, the magistrate of Wuhu County, received an order from the province to clean up all public properties in the county. Sun has convened various groups in the county to organize a public property cleanup committee, which is scheduled to be established on the 14th to clean up separately.

Small steamships operating in Wuhu, Neihe, Nanling, Xuanzhou, and other places are now experiencing higher water levels than in previous years due to the backflow of the river tide and the influx of mountain floods. The dikes along the river are in imminent danger. All small steamships have successively suspended operations in compliance with customs restrictions.

The Wuhu Tongji Ferry Company, recognizing that there are thousands of people traveling between the north and south banks of the Yangtze River in Wuhu every day, and that small boats are dangerous due to the wide river surface, purchased small steamships to start a ferry service. Previously, a dispute arose with the "Zhenjie" rowing gang, and the ferry service was suspended again. Later, the Municipal Affairs Office convened several meetings and decided that the ferry company would subsidize the interests of the rowing gang before the service was peacefully restored. However, yesterday, the pontoon of the ferry's north bank dock was suddenly destroyed, causing the ferry service to stop again. The Municipal Affairs Office, which had been collecting municipal donations from passengers since the ferry service was established, was obliged to mediate. (9th)

Shanghai National Goods Touring Group Arrives in Qingdao

Qingdao City Holds National Goods Exhibition

Qingdao Correspondence: This national goods exhibition in Qingdao is unprecedented in North China. The Shanghai National Goods Touring Group, with more than 100 members, also arrived in Qingdao a few days ago to prepare for participation. At 10:00 AM today (the 7th), party and government organs and representatives from all walks of life gathered at the Qi Yan Hall to hold the opening ceremony of the National Goods Exhibition Hall and the National Goods Exhibition. The presidium consisted of Mayor Ge Jingen, Municipal Steering Committee member Yang Xingqin, Social Affairs Bureau Director Yang Jin, General Chamber of Commerce member Ding Jingchen, and Shanghai National Goods Touring Group Chairman Chen Pengru. After the opening meeting, Chairman Yang Jin reported first, stating that the National Goods Exhibition Hall was reorganized from the former Commodity Exhibition Hall and had been in preparation for several months. The opening could not be held earlier because the national goods solicited from various places had not arrived completely. Although the exhibits had not all arrived, they were mostly ready. As for the National Goods Exhibition, it was scheduled to be held once a year according to the regulations of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, on the one hand, to let the public know how many national goods there were, and on the other hand, for the government to reward them. But the current exhibition was a kind of national goods mobile exhibition. This kind of exhibition had been held in Jiangsu Province several times, and the results were very good. The first was the "China Exhibition" held in Shanghai by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce the year before last. The largest was last year's "West Lake Exhibition," and the most recent was last month's "Nanjing Silk Exhibition." Henan, Hunan, Zhenjiang, Suzhou, and Hangzhou had also held exhibitions. Because of historical reasons, Qingdao City was flooded with foreign goods and had few national goods, so it was urgent to promote them. After this exhibition, the Chinese people would know the benefits of national goods and would use national goods, which would not be in vain for today's meeting. Then, Committee Member Yang and Mayor Ge gave speeches. Finally, Shanghai National Goods Touring Group Chairman Chen Peng reported that the group had originally planned to go to Guangdong first, but because they received a letter from the Qingdao Social Affairs Bureau inviting them to Qingdao, they decided to come to Qingdao first to participate in the promotion. He was grateful for the guidance of all parties. Regarding manufacturing, he would strive for excellence after returning to Shanghai to meet the expectations of the people. The significance of this tour was to conduct practical investigations into the needs of the people in various places and then seek the development of national goods. After the closing meeting, the entire group went to the National Goods Exhibition Hall together to hold the opening ceremony, then went to each exhibition room to visit various national goods samples and take photos as souvenirs. At that time, the number of people who came to view and shop had already been unceasing. It was found that a total of 36 factories had come to Qingdao this time. The names of each factory and the types of products were investigated as follows: Shengde Weaving Factory (silk fabrics, artificial ivory chopsticks), Gongzu Footwear Factory (silk socks), Zhenhua Pottery Factory (Yixing pottery), Huayang Dyeing and Weaving Factory (cloth), Ruyi Xiang Factory (silverware), Dahua Industrial Factory (thread crepe silk), Liyong Pottery Factory (Yixing pottery), Peide Tie and Shirt Factory (shirts and ties), Huadong Manufacturing Factory (Huadong crepe), Yao Chuanhong Lacquerware Factory (art lacquerware), May 30th National Goods Company (Hangzhou paper umbrellas), Guangshengyuan Food Company (candies and food), Wuzhou Guben Medicine Soap Factory (cosmetics and medicines), West Lake Tea Factory (tea and lotus root flour), Brothers Industrial Society (cosmetics), Senyuanxiang Jewelry Factory (jewelry), Yuan Zhenhe Silk Factory (silk fabrics), Chen Yuanxing Comb Factory (Changzhou combs), Longxingxiang Copper Factory (copperware), Chunhua Silk Factory (silk fabrics), Lin Rattanware Factory (rattan willow ware), Dacheng Weaving Factory (cotton silk fabrics), New World Umbrella Factory (umbrellas), Zhenhua Paint Company (Flying Tiger paint), Xiangtai Manufacturing Factory (silk undershirts, socks, and pants), China Celluloid Factory (tableware), Qida Silk Weaving Factory (silk woven scenery), Nanyang Tobacco Company (cigarettes), Qiming Dyeing and Weaving Factory (cloth), Yapuer Electric Bulb Factory (light bulbs), China Enamel Factory (enamelware), Taikang Food Company (canned food), Meixia Silk Factory (silk fabrics), Samsung Cotton Iron Factory (cotton fabrics, towels), Dafeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory (cloth), Dazhong Towel Factory (towels), Baofa Sauce Essence Factory (soy sauce essence), Wuhe Manufacturing Factory (cotton fabrics) (July 7th)

Hangzhou Express Letter

Serious bandit alerts have been repeatedly reported in Jiande County, and rumors are rampant. Several hundred people from the county have come to Hangzhou to seek temporary shelter. The province has dispatched the third regiment of the Security Team, led by Zhu, to suppress the bandits. They have departed in batches over the past few days.

Lanxi, in eastern Zhejiang, is a region specializing in ham and cured meat production. The Department of Finance has proposed to increase the donation rate. Industry colleagues have elected representatives from Yuanfa to telegram a request for exemption in order to alleviate business difficulties. Yesterday, a reply was received stating that ham and cured meat are not essential foods, as everyone knows, and are classified as semi-luxury goods. The added tax is very small. If the industry can pay attention to improving the quality of products and sell them overseas, they will be welcomed. There is no need to worry about the encroachment of American and Japanese hams. Please advise and explain in detail, and do not hesitate and wait and see.

There are fourteen banks in Hangzhou, including the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Local Bank, Industrial Bank, Xingye Bank, Huidi Bank, Chufeng Bank, Dianye Bank, Savings Bank, Daoyi Bank, Salt Bank, Continental Bank, Agricultural and Industrial Bank, and Central Bank. The industry originally established a guild, which was canceled long ago. Now, the Bank of China, Local Bank, Huidi Bank, Xingye Bank, and other banks have initiated the legal organization of a trade association, which is currently in preparation.

The Department of Finance received a telegram from the Jiaxing Unified Donation Bureau requesting instructions on whether Minfeng Paper Company's machine-made Western-style paper goods could be exempted from donations. It was found that Minfeng Paper Factory was established on the old site of Hefeng and Jincheng factories, and the paper produced was machine-made and imitated Western goods. It should be handled in accordance with the previous case of Hefeng and Jincheng factories, allowing exemption from donations. The waste paper from raw materials can also be exempted from donations in accordance with the previous case of Jincheng Factory. The Ministry of Finance will also be consulted for instructions. Local Communications

Songjiang

Summary of County Government County Administration Meeting: The County Government held its 65th County Administration Meeting yesterday, chaired by County Magistrate Jin. Matters discussed: (1) The Public Security Bureau submitted a case stating that the drum towers in the four cities were old and dilapidated and would collapse, requesting demolition to avoid danger. It was decided that the county magistrate should order the Construction Bureau to investigate and estimate the demolition costs and the price of old materials to offset the profits and losses and submit a report for review. (2) The Construction Bureau proposed that the city gates of the four cities were old and dilapidated, severely corroded, and difficult to open and close. Now that the barbican has been demolished, it should be repaired urgently to strengthen the city's defenses. All the construction costs are planned to be offset by the wood from the barbican city gate. If there is a shortfall, it will be supplemented by the bricks and stones from the demolition of the barbican. Is it feasible to ask for a public decision? It was decided that the county magistrate should order the Construction Bureau to estimate the price and submit a report for review.

Rice Merchants Association Limits Price for Fair Sale: The Rice Merchants Association of this city was previously advised by the county government to limit the price and sell at a fair price. Later, out of consideration for public opinion and the poor, they all agreed to automatically sell at a fair price. Yesterday, a meeting was held at the County Chamber of Commerce to first vote on which method was more appropriate, fair price or rice distribution. It was unanimously decided to sell at a fair price. It was then decided that the limited price of Du rice should not exceed 21 yuan per shi, and Xiang rice should be sold at a price reduction of two yuan per city price. A total of 4,000 yuan was allocated to open sales in the three temples of Dongmen, Cangqiao, and other four bureaus. Each person could buy from one jin to ten jin without needing a certificate to maintain the livelihood of small artisans. The fair sale was held at the same time as the government-regulated fair price period. After the general discussion, a committee meeting was held today to discuss the detailed rules of the affair and was named the Songjiang Rice Merchants Association Fair Price Office, which has already been prepared and is in progress.

Mother and Son Killed by Train: Yesterday (the 11th), the first express train from Shanghai to Beijing drove to Yangqiao outside Qimen. A mother and son, whose names were unknown, were walking on the bridge and could not avoid being hit by the wheels and falling into the river, where they were injured and killed. Kunshan

Stolen Ancient Paintings Recovered: Xu Wuqi, a former gentleman in Dongtang Street in the city, had a large collection of Yuan and Ming ancient paintings. Last month, more than ten ancient paintings were suddenly stolen by thieves. The value was huge. He immediately reported to the County Public Security Bureau for investigation. Wei, the chief of the Criminal Investigation Department, learned that the ancient paintings were stolen by Yao Gengquan, a carpenter in the case. He immediately sent detectives to arrest him. The criminal had already fled after hearing the news. Yao's father, Longhai, was arrested for the case. According to his confession, he was instigated by two Wu brothers who were at large. According to his confession, Chief Wei immediately presented Yao to the county government on the tenth and continued to strictly arrest the Wu brothers who were at large and bring them to justice.

Another Kidnapping Case in Qidun Township: At about 1:00 AM the night before last, two bandit ships suddenly arrived at Taojiaqiao in Qidun Township of the County Bureau. There were more than ten bandits on board, each with guns and weapons. After landing, they entered Chen Yushu's house and kidnapped Chen's two grandsons from the bed without asking why and took them to the ship. They then went to Xu Jianxian's house and kidnapped Xu, declaring that they needed to prepare 10,000 yuan to redeem them at a certain place. The bandit ship passed through Nantangdun Village and kidnapped two Yao children. Afterwards, each master reported to the fourth district chief, Zhu Wenyuan, requesting him to forward the report to the county government for strict arrest.

Wujiang

Passenger Dies of Heat Stroke at Wharf: Zhao Baochang, a 46-year-old from Huzhou, Zhejiang, came to Jiang from Shanghai a few days ago to visit the family members of his former master, Qian Gang. He stayed at the Hongan Hotel on Beizha Street. On the morning of the ninth, Zhao Chenzhou went to the Beimen wharf to return to Huzhou. Unexpectedly, Zhao contracted a sudden illness due to the hot weather and died of heat stroke at the wharf. The sanitation officer checked and telegraphed the county government, which sent someone from Suzhou to inspect and confirmed that he had died of illness. His belongings, such as a rattan basket, were left in the county, awaiting the burial of the body, and a telegram was sent to Zhao's nephew, Xu Guisheng, in the Taihefang of Huzhou, to come to Jiang to collect and bury him.

Provincial Party Department Lecture Group Arrives in Jiang: The Jiangsu Provincial Party Department's Wei lecture group arrived in Jiang from Suzhou on the tenth. The county party department welcomed them and arranged everything. It was decided to give lectures in Pingwang on the eleventh and go to Shengze on the twelfth and return to the province on the thirteenth.

Wuxi

Change of Police Chief: Huang Zhenbai, the Wuxi County Police Chief, has served since his appointment for almost five months. Recently, due to the overwhelming workload of handling wounded soldiers' reception, and the various criticisms arising from the conscription of laborers, Huang specifically submitted a request to the county government, which was forwarded to the provincial government, firmly requesting to resign from his post. The Department of Civil Affairs approved the recommendation to appoint Xu Jiugui, the current secretary of the Provincial Public Security Bureau, to fill the vacancy. He is expected to come to Wuxi next week for the handover.

Water Police Pay Attention to Lake Defense: The seventh team of the Second District of the Lake Water Police, originally stationed in the Mudu area, recently, its captain, Li Jianxun, considered that the towns of Xukou and Guangfu in Suzhou are important passes of Taihu Lake. In light of the Guoxiang Town incident of killing officials and seizing weapons, it is urgent to take precautions. He specially requested Chief Mao to transfer the first squad originally stationed in Guangfu to Xukou, and the third squad originally stationed in Xihua Town to Guangfu, to strengthen lake defense. Chief Mao, based on the report, has forwarded it to the Department of Civil Affairs for review.

Case of One Boat, Four Lives Solved: Mao Mujun, the district chief of the Second District of the Provincial Public Security Team stationed on the water in Wuxi, recently received a secret report stating that the bandits Qian Genbao, Wang Kunshou, and Wang Yinlong, who murdered Xu Jianshan, a villager from Kaihua Township, and Shao Qiaosheng, a boatman, and his sons Guoqing and Qiqing, were hiding in Guangfu Town, Wuxian County. He requested the dispatch of police to arrest them. Chief Mao, upon receiving the report, immediately ordered detective chief Ni Gusheng to lead detectives to investigate. When they arrived at the location, they saw three fishing boats and knew they were not good people. They bravely went forward, but the bandits on the fishing boats dared to open fire and resist arrest. As a result, the bandits were outnumbered and finally captured by Detective Ni, who arrested the three bandits Qian Genbao, Wang Kunshou, and Wang Yinlong, and seized the three fishing boats together. They were escorted to Wuxi yesterday to be sent to the district for interrogation.

Opium Smuggler Arrested and Sent to the Bureau: Cao Afu, a local resident, has been engaged in opium smuggling for a long time. His son, Jingqing, is deeply addicted to opium. The other day, the Public Security Bureau sent detectives to search his house. The detectives went upstairs and saw Cao's son, Jingqing, lying on a couch, smoking opium. The detectives arrested Cao Jingqing and took him to the bureau along with the evidence. Then they arrested Cao Afu. However, it has been three days since they were taken to the bureau and they have not yet been transferred to the county government for interrogation.

Changzhou

County Government Convened a Meeting to Organize Low-Price Grain Sales: The Wuyi County government convened a meeting at the Chamber of Commerce at 2 PM on the 10th to discuss preparations for low-price grain sales. More than ten representatives from various agencies attended. Xu Wenjun, the chairman of the County Party Rectification Association, was elected as the chairman. After the report, various issues were discussed: (1) It was decided to purchase No. 3 wheat flour for low-price sales. (2) It was decided that a second preparatory meeting would be held at the County Chamber of Commerce at 3 PM on July 13th, as the economy must be secured before the event can be held. Each agency must formulate specific plans for discussion and decision-making at that time.

Carpenters' Strike: Wuyi County carpenters demanded a 30% increase in wages from shop owners due to the rising cost of living, referencing the precedent set by the bricklayers. The carpenters' original wages were 60 cents per day, and a 30% increase would bring it to 78 cents. The shop owners only agreed to add 10 cents per day for rice subsidies. After repeated negotiations, both parties submitted requests to the county government and the Construction Bureau for review. The carpenters, seeing no decision made by the 10th, went on strike.

Carpentry Hook Workers Resume Work: The Wuyi County carpentry hook workers demanded a 20% wage increase. After striking for many days without success, the Carpentry Guild decided to change the temporary rice subsidy. Each contractor first acknowledged that the hook workers would receive a 20% increase based on the original price starting from July 15th, and work would resume immediately. All workers unanimously agreed and invited representatives from various ports to come to Changzhou on the 20th of this month to discuss increasing water fees.

Zhenjiang

Department Assigns Investigator to Examine Public Property in Four Counties: Hu Pu'an, the director of the Jiangsu Department of Civil Affairs, appointed Yu Youren, the director of the Provincial Relief Institute, to investigate the public property issues in Liyang, Jintan, Danyang, and Zhenjiang counties, to provide a basis for handling the matter.

Floating Corpses Found Along the River: Yesterday, two floating corpses were found upstream of the Xiashamatou in Shunjiang Township, which belongs to the county. The Baoshantang of the township funded the dispatch of fishing boats to retrieve them. One was a male corpse, about 30 years old, resembling a worker, wearing a blue cloth short shirt and trousers, and Yuan cloth shoes. The other was a female corpse, about 20 years old, wearing a white gauze jacket, Yuan-colored gauze trousers, and dark-colored socks, and Yuan cloth shoes. Her ears had a pair of gold earrings. The Baoshantang provided coffins for both of them for proper burial, awaiting family members to claim them. It is said that these two floating corpses came from Jiaxing Bridge or were passengers of the Puji Wheel, but it is unknown.

Continuation of the Kidnapping Case at Hujia Bridge: The ringleader of the case where Hu Sui and others from Hujia Bridge in the eastern countryside were kidnapped has been apprehended. After the county government dispatched police to Xinfeng to recover the hostages and arrest the key criminal, Gu Jinbiao, who was interrogated and sentenced to death, the ringleader of the case, Zhai Wanquan, had been at large for a long time. Yesterday, Zhai suddenly sneaked back to the village and was discovered by the county government's bailiffs while fishing at the fishing platform by the lake outside the West Gate. He has now been escorted to the county for interrogation.

Announcement of Women's Organization Committee Members: The Women's Association of this county has been suspended for a long time. It is now instructed that the revenue and expenditure of the county's budget for the 19th year are still difficult to match, and it is claimed that the expenses of all agencies are paid at 85%. Suspected Thieves Escorted to the County for Interrogation: The Second Garrison of the Public Security Bureau of Sanguan Township, together with the Detective Team, arrested eight suspected thieves in various villages: Zhou Lincai, Zhang Lingen, Meng Fanglin, Xu Linbao, Ma Jinkang, Yang Hongchao, Yang Hongbao, and Chen Tongbao. Yang Hongbao and Chen Tongbao were released on bail. The remaining six, Zhou Lincai and others, were escorted to the Public Security Bureau on the 10th and sent to the county for interrogation.

Nantong

Military Department Sends Personnel to Discuss Establishing a Wounded Soldiers' Hospital: The Ministry of Military Affairs sent Wang Shanqing to Nantong to discuss with the county government the establishment of a rear wounded soldiers' hospital, which should be able to accommodate 1,300 people. Liu Jianxiang and others accompanied Wang to inspect various locations, but none were suitable. Representatives from all sectors of the community presented to Wang the facts that Nantong's strength is lacking, food is scarce, and there is no one to provide treatment and care, and that reactionary factions are constantly causing disturbances. They requested permission to postpone the establishment in accordance with the letter from the General Headquarters Staff Office. Wang agreed to return to the Ministry for instructions.

Flood Relief Project Along the River: The dikes along the Yao and Wang ports of Nantong collapsed due to river tides, causing a flood disaster. The Department of Construction sent Pei Yixiang to Nantong to investigate. Since the flood season has arrived and the river tide has risen sharply, the situation is particularly dangerous. The county government ordered the Finance Bureau to allocate 4,000 yuan to carry out emergency repairs as needed and began construction immediately.

Police Team Intercepts Large Quantity of Opium and Poison Pills: The Yugang Maritime Police team intercepted a sand boat at 11 PM on the 9th, seized a box of opium and more than 100,000 red and white poison pills, and arrested the smuggler Zhu, who was sent to the county court for trial.

Commander of Anti-Banditry in Nine Counties Removed: Li Changjiang, the commander of the Provincial Police Corps, who was previously concurrently appointed by the Provincial Government as the commander of anti-banditry in nine counties in Jiangbei, requested the Provincial Government to revoke the concurrent position because the anti-banditry cases were being handled simultaneously throughout the province and he was naturally responsible.

Jingjiang

Thieves Escorted to Suzhou for Retrial: The county government arrested eight thieves: Gao Mingguang, Miao Chungeng, You Shenglan, Lu Laosan, Chen Yiqing, Chang Kouyu, Chang Laojiu, and Xu Heguan. They confessed to robbery outside the county and were sentenced to imprisonment of varying degrees by the county government according to the severity of the crimes. The criminals refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the High Court, which was approved. The court hearing was scheduled for July 16th. The county government escorted the criminals to Suzhou yesterday to await trial.

Three Families Robbed in One Night in Dajue Town: On the evening of July 7th, more than ten thieves armed with guns and flashlights broke into the house of Zhu Jinyuan, beat Jinyuan, and then held Jinyuan's son and his brother Erlang, demanding silver dollars. They immediately took out 30 yuan, but the thieves were still not satisfied and continued to demand more. The whole family pleaded that they really had no money to give. The thieves, angered, shot and killed Erlang and Jinyuan's son, and then went to Miao Zhuangshu's house in Xujiatai to rob. The losses were relatively light.

Huzhou

Xu Xiaoli's Home Robbed Twice in One Night: A resident named Xu Xiaoli in Chang'anli, outside the West Gate of Changxing, was working as a clerk in a cloth store in the city. A few days ago, he received a letter from bandits demanding 500 yuan to be handed over at a certain place. Xu ignored it because he did not have such a large sum of money. Suddenly, on the evening of the 7th, more than ten bandits armed with guns and speaking with a Henan accent broke into the door. Xu knew something was wrong and escaped to the back. The bandits went inside and arbitrarily searched and looted all the clothes, rice, and other items. Unexpectedly, the next morning, the same bandits came again and went straight in through the front door to the bedroom and fired two shots. Xu knew he could not avoid it, so he came out from behind the curtain and knelt down, begging repeatedly, and took out 50 yuan in banknotes and handed it over. The bandits then fired a warning shot and left.

Bandits Rob in Broad Daylight: Shen Anbao, a resident of Fancun in the southwestern countryside of Wuxing, had been cutting trees for others in the mountains of Heping. On the 8th of this month, he was carrying a bag of clothes home. At about 2 PM, about three miles away from Hejiabu, he suddenly encountered two bandits in short clothes blocking his way. They took out handguns and forbade him from making a sound. Shen Anbao had no choice but to let them search him and take all his eight yuan in cash, a dozen small yuan, five pieces of clothing, and a quilted blanket.

Pinghu

Two More Robbery Cases in the Eastern Countryside: At 1 AM on the morning of the 7th, more than twenty bandits came from the direction of Quan Gong Pavilion in the southeast of the Xulifu family in Xielefang Gaojia Bridge. They broke into the house with weapons and tied up the head of the household's wife, robbing extensively. Lifu and his nephew Zhijian escaped through the back wall. They stole 15 yuan in banknotes, gold jewelry, and many pieces of clothing. The family of Ding Sidi, a farmer near Yaqian Town, who was relatively well-off, was robbed by 20 to 30 bandits at midnight on the 7th. Sidi was tied up and tortured. More than 100 silver dollars and clothes and ornaments worth 600 to 700 gold were stolen.

Conflict Between Salt Smugglers and Salt Police: Liu Xiaohe, the captain of the Third Team of the Business-Run Anti-Smuggling Camp, led three patrol boats to moor near Zhoujiawei on the 8th. Unexpectedly, a large group of private salt empty boats passed by at night. Seeing the patrol boats, the salt smugglers landed ashore with guns and opened fire. Captain Liu was unprepared due to the suddenness of the incident, resulting in three policemen being wounded. It is now reported that the captain has escorted the injured policemen to the Jiaxing camp headquarters for treatment and is investigating the origins of the salt smugglers in order to punish them.

Jiaxing

Department Orders Investigation of Complaint Against Public Security Bureau Chief: Mo Runxun, the chief of the Jiaxing Public Security Bureau, has been repeatedly complained about by local groups for improper measures. Recently, due to a major case, the victim's family and business associations have filed complaints with the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, the Zhejiang Provincial Government, and the Department of Civil Affairs. It is now reported that the Department of Civil Affairs has ordered the Jiaxing County Government to investigate and report back for review. However, public opinion is skeptical of the department's order to the county government to investigate, and they are continuing to request the Department of Civil Affairs to send someone else to investigate in order to ensure fairness.

Jiashan

Boat Capsizes and Three Die: In the Xuejiayang area of ​​the Western Countryside, yesterday, a cargo boat belonging to Bu Asan was carrying goods through the area when it collided with a Mashan boat coming from the opposite direction. The collision caused the boat to capsize, resulting in the drowning of Bu's adopted son Er Mao, his daughter San Nv, and his infant child. The body of the infant child has not yet been recovered.

Xiaoshan

Disturbances Caused by Forced Donations by Village Farmers' Associations: The farmers' associations in the four townships of Xiaoshan have recently been collecting membership fees, ranging from four cents to one dime per person per month. Recently, they have been adding special donations of five or ten yuan to those who appear to be better off. The farmers cannot bear the burden. At this busy time for farmers, they often borrow the power of the farmers' associations to intimidate them. Their evil methods are even worse than the previous forced rice collection by evil landlords. Such extortion has been discovered in Dongcaodun, Shu, and other villages. It is reported that farmers have sent representatives to the provincial government to appeal for help. It is unknown how the provincial government will support the farmers.

Investigation and Punishment of Illegal Activities by Two Village Chiefs: Xu Nailian, the village chief of Wutu Village in Xiaoshan, illegally collected report fees of two dimes and two cents per mu when handling land reports, which violated provincial orders. After Sun Yuanshun and others filed a complaint with the provincial and county governments, County Magistrate Du sent someone to secretly investigate and found that it was true. He has been handed over to the court for prosecution. Xu Bingkui, the village chief of Xuanling Village, was dismissed and investigated by the county government for fraudulent low-price grain sales.

Arrest and Public Display of Thieves Who Kidnap and Steal Low-Price Grain Coupons: Since the opening of low-price grain sales in Xiaoshan on June 5, some kidnappers and thieves have been deceiving women and children to seize their profits. On the 7th, a thief named Xu Zigen defrauded a villager of two yuan and a low-price grain coupon, falsely claiming to buy rice from the low-price grain bureau on his behalf, never to return. The villager reported to the police, who arrested him near the motor road. He was immediately displayed to the public at the low-price grain bureau, paraded through the streets for a day, and then released.

Japanese Swimming Making Great Strides

Two Years of Preparation and Hard Training

The Sole Purpose is World Hegemony

(Special Correspondent) The Japanese Aquatic Sports Federation held a board meeting on July 5 to prepare for this year's championship. The meeting concluded that, in light of recent surprising progress, such as reducing the 1500 meters to 19 minutes, the 400 meters to 5 minutes, and breaking 2 minutes and 20 seconds for the 200 meters, and with a number of emerging talents, it is optimistic about winning the 1500-meter and 800-meter relay swimming championships at the World Olympics to be held in two years. As for the Olympic men's swimming events, which are the 100-meter, 400-meter, 1500-meter freestyle, 100-meter backstroke, 200-meter breaststroke, and 800-meter relay, the United States specializes in freestyle and backstroke, but the breaststroke is not as good as Japan's, Germany's or the Philippines', so Japan is determined to work hard to encourage the old and new to train diligently. There is great hope of seizing world swimming hegemony. With ambitious aspirations thundering, the next competition is a golden opportunity. They advocated two years of training preparation with the Olympics as the primary goal. In the future, various competition events will focus on the World Championship events. The entire venue unanimously decided to actively work hard and forge ahead.

The British Boxing Board of Control declared that it does not recognize Schmeling's acquisition of the world heavyweight championship. German sports circles were surprised. Six Female Generals to the Czech Republic on July 25th

London Will Have

New Style of British Football

The London Howard Enterprise Group, known for its efforts to promote sports, is now planning to introduce a new style of six-a-side soccer and is preparing to test the match between Leyton and Galston in Layton next month. An agreement has also been reached, and they are actively working with the relations of the White City and Wembley stadiums to promote this skill.

This new style of soccer is organized with six players per team, one goalkeeper, one defender, and three forwards. During the match, all members, referees, and linesmen wear masks and plan to provide bonuses to attract top players to participate. They now want to use four courts to hold a championship with a reward of 1,000 pounds for the final to attract the interest of the audience.

The teams plan to use playing cards as their representative names. If the negotiations with Wembley are successful, Wembley will be named "Ace", White City will be named "King", Galston will be named "Queen", and Layton will be named "Jacks". Each team takes turns playing against each other. The field is 80 yards long and 60 yards wide. The match time is usually 90 minutes, which is divided into 15 minutes. However, shots are only allowed to be scored from within the penalty line. If the two teams are tied, the winner is determined by the number of corner kicks.

According to Howard, who promotes this new style of soccer, many stars are now willing to participate. Although the members wear masks for the first test run, their true identities will be revealed in the future.

However, the Football Association stipulates that players are not allowed to participate in six-a-side exhibition matches after the end of the season. Those who violate this will be subject to exile and removal. As for those who promote this new game, they claim that they are confident that they can solicit first-class players and will never extend their membership to any team. Moreover, many stars have signed up to serve at any time, and the competition can be held at any time. They firmly believe that this new style of six-a-side soccer will definitely develop and succeed in the future.

Women's One Mile

New World Record in Swimming

Ms. Madison, a seventeen-year-old student from California, USA, set a new world record for the women's one-mile freestyle swim at the Long Beach Swimming Championships with a time of 24 minutes and 34.2 seconds. The previous record of 24 minutes and 49 seconds was held by Ms. McKim since 1928. Ms. Madison also set a new freestyle record in four events at the Jacksonville, Florida, meet in March of this year, greatly impressing the women's swimming world and establishing her as a rising star.

YMCA Sponsored

Handball Championship Concludes

Group A Champion: Hong Yu Kui

Group B Champion: Hong Ru Lin

Group C Champion: Cheng Zhen Hua

Challenge Match to be Held Next Friday

The YMCA-sponsored Shanghai Singles Handball Championship was divided into three groups (A, B, and C), with enthusiastic participation. Hong E Qing, Gu Yong Zhao, and Zhu Kuan were appointed as committee members, with Ling Xi Tao as the general secretary. The event concluded successfully, with players displaying spirited and persistent efforts throughout the competition. The final matches for each group were held at the YMCA handball court yesterday afternoon at 5:30 PM, drawing a large and enthusiastic crowd. Hong Yu Kui defeated Sun Dao Sheng to win the Group A championship, Hong Ru Lin defeated Lu Ai Bai to win the Group B championship, and Cheng Zhen Hua defeated Luo Shun Da to win the Group C championship. The results of each group are summarized below:

Group A: Hong Yu Kui Defeats Sun Dao Sheng

11-1, 11-9, 11-9

At 5:30 PM, Hong and Sun of Group A took to the stage. Both players were highly skilled. Sun, the veteran, played aggressively, winning the first game 11-1, seemingly poised to seize the championship. However, his stamina waned, and he became fatigued. Hong, young and strong, with vigorous energy, attacked from both sides, overwhelming Sun. Hong won the next two games 11-9, 11-9, reversing the situation to win the championship. Sun's loss was due to a lack of physical strength, not a lack of fighting spirit. The referees were Zhu Kuan and Ling Xi Tao, and the recorder was Chen Yu Zhang.

Group B: Hong Ru Lin Defeats Lu Ai Bai

22-20, 21-9

After the Group A match, the Group B match began, featuring Hong Ru Lin against Lu Ai Bai. Hong is the brother of Group A champion Hong Yu Kui and is also highly skilled. He maintained momentum after the game started. Lu Ai Bai showed some resistance, however, the tension of the hard game continued to mount. Hong won the first game 22-20. In the second game, Hong's momentum increased, and he became unstoppable, while Lu's form deteriorated, losing 21-9. Hong Ru Lin won the championship 2-0.

Group C: Cheng Zhen Hua Defeats Luo Shun Da

21-14, 21-3

Cheng Zhen Hua won the Group C championship effortlessly. Cheng's skill is so advanced that he could easily stand out even in Group B. His opponent, Luo Shun Da, although defeated, fought hard and persevered until the end. The scores were 21-14, 21-3.

Challenge Match Next Friday

General Zhu Kuan to Compete

A Challenge Contest will be held next Friday. General Zhu Kuan will compete against Group A champion Hong Yu Kui. Group A runner-up Sun Dao Sheng will compete against Group B champion Hong Ru Lin. Group B runner-up Lu Ai Bai will compete against Group C champion Cheng Zhen Hua. It will be a clash of talents, a battle of equals, promising a grand spectacle and a new era for handball in Shanghai.

Ministry of Education Strictly Limits Private School Registration

The Ministry of Education has clearly set deadlines for the registration of private schools at all levels in all regions and has issued instructions for compliance. The Ministry has instructed education departments in each province and municipality to investigate the large number of private schools at all levels in their areas. The Ministry has repeatedly ordered these schools to register according to regulations. Some schools have submitted registration applications, but others are waiting to see what happens. This delay is unacceptable and should be strictly addressed by setting clear deadlines to ensure compliance. The deadline for registration of private schools at all levels in the capital is the end of this summer vacation, i.e., before the start of the first semester of the 19th year of the Republic, as previously ordered by the Ministry. The registration deadline for all other private schools should be determined by the education departments of each province and municipality, taking into account the specific circumstances. The deadline should be no later than the end of the next summer vacation, i.e., the day before the start of the first semester of the 20th year of the Republic. Schools that fail to register by the deadline should be ordered by the education departments of each province and municipality to suspend enrollment or close down. However, private schools in military, disaster, or remote areas that are unable to register on time due to special circumstances may have their deadlines extended by the education departments of each province and municipality with the approval of the Ministry.

Recovering Education Rights in Concessions

Shanghai Municipal Government to Find Ways

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau previously petitioned the Ministry of Education to request the recovery of education rights in concessions. The Ministry of Education forwarded the petition to the Executive Yuan and sent a letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has now replied to the Ministry of Education, stating that it would be easier to recover education rights in concessions if the Shanghai Municipal Government negotiated with the concession authorities to find remedies. It is reported that the Ministry of Education has consulted the Shanghai Municipal Government.

County Education Bureau Plans to Increase Education Funding for This Year

Plans to Add a Percentage from Salt Price Increase

The plan is currently under discussion.

The Shanghai County Education Bureau believes that the county's land tax has already been increased to 16 cents per mu, imposing a heavy burden on farmers, and that further increases are difficult. However, increased education funding is necessary. It is proposed that the county, together with nearby counties, request an additional percentage of the salt price increase for education funding this year. Other possible sources of funding are being explored. The plan is currently under discussion and will be submitted to the provincial authorities for approval after a decision has been made.

Strict Enrollment at Wuben Girls' Middle School

The Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School has a long history and a high reputation in society. The current principal is Wang Xiaoying. At the beginning of the school year, the entrance examination for new students is very strict. Graduates of the school's elementary and junior high schools with academic performance in the top grade can directly enter the corresponding grade. All others must undergo the same examination procedures as new students. The percentage of continuing students is generally 27%, while the percentage of new students is 73%. The school hopes to achieve uniform academic standards and practical learning within three years. Seven or eight hundred people applied for the exam this time. The exams for the first and second grades of junior high school were completed in one day, and the exams for the first and second grades of senior high school were held over two days. Yesterday was the first day of the new student exams. There were six examination rooms, all sealed, with strict invigilation and a solemn atmosphere. Although the weather was hot and candidates were sweating profusely, their spirits were high as they competed for this one day. The results will be announced after evaluation. The second examination period is expected to be in mid-August.
