City Public Works Bureau Bans Dog Racing Ads

The City Public Works Bureau, considering dog racing to be a form of gambling, has strictly prohibited the posting of dog racing advertisements to prevent them from poisoning society and causing endless harm. It previously sent a letter to the French Tramway and Electric Light Company instructing them to remove dog racing advertisements posted on French trams. The company replied that the advertisements were only posted on trams within the French Concession and that they had notified the British company not to display them on trams operating in the Chinese area. However, it has recently been found that French Route 6 trams are again carrying dog racing advertisements in the Chinese area, which is considered a violation of the ban. Therefore, another letter has been sent to the French company requesting that they remove the advertisements immediately to uphold the law.

Inaugural Meeting of the National Medicine Trade Association

The inaugural meeting of the Shanghai National Medicine Trade Association was held yesterday at the Ningbo Fellow-Provincials Association on Xizang Road. The meeting began promptly at 9:00 AM with the ringing of a bell. Zhang Meian, Cen Zhiliang, and Zhuang Meitang were elected as the presidium. The chairman gave a speech outlining the purpose of the meeting, and the preparatory committee reported on the progress of the preparations.

The articles of association were approved, and the first executive committee was elected. The results were announced on the spot: Cen Zhiliang received 94 votes, Zhang Meian received 82 votes, Cen Qisheng and Zhang Hongzhao each received 72 votes, Chen Chuxiang and Zhuang Meitang each received 71 votes, Tong Guangfu received 69 votes, Chen Tiansheng received 68 votes, Feng Jinpu received 61 votes, Sun Wenan received 59 votes, Cen Binghuang received 55 votes, Zhou Gansheng received 54 votes, and Niu Hegao and Li Kangnian each received 50 votes, and Guo Baosheng received 47 votes. The above 15 people were elected as executive committee members. Fei Shenqi, Zhou Zhide, Ge Kejian, Wang Quanmei, and Zhang Zhihao, in order of votes received, were elected as alternate executive committee members. The elected executive committee members took their oaths of office under the supervision of representatives from various organizations and assumed their positions immediately. Representatives from higher authorities delivered instructions, guests gave speeches, and proposals were discussed. (A) Regarding the issue of how to proceed with the revision of labor-management conditions as instructed by the Central Executive Committee, it was resolved to adopt the draft prepared by the preparatory committee and submit it to the executive committee for active handling. (B) Regarding the issue of promptly establishing service regulations for employees in the industry to facilitate compliance and emphasize store rules, it was resolved to combine it with Proposal A for joint handling. (C) Regarding the issue of properly discussing and establishing industry regulations, it was resolved to submit it to the executive committee for discussion and implementation. (D) Member representative Zhang Meian proposed that the industry should establish a national medicine specialty school and hospital to promote talent cultivation and construction.

Page 16

It was resolved to approve and implement the proposal. Gu Huijun proposed that the industry should follow the national calendar and abolish the lunar calendar's New Moon discounts, which was seconded by Fang Chang'an and others. It was resolved to submit it to the executive committee for review. Zhang Zhihao proposed whether individual members of the former industry's merchant association should still belong to the trade association, which should be discussed. It was resolved to submit it to the executive committee for interpretation by higher authorities. Chen Tiansheng proposed that the association should designate the Yaohuang Temple as its headquarters and incorporate it into the articles of association, which was resolved to approve. The chairman delivered a speech of thanks, and a photograph was taken. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM. The elected executive committee members were scheduled to hold their first meeting at the association today to mutually elect the chairman, standing committee members, and department directors, and to discuss the cases referred by the general assembly.

A Husband's Immorality Leads to Divorce Through Mediation by Both Families

Xu Zuquan, a resident of Nanxujiawan, Wusong, has a daughter named Xiuling, 21 years old. She is intelligent, beautiful, and virtuous. Zuquan loves her very much. In the autumn of last year, he arranged for her to marry Zhang Songbao's son, Lin Geng, from Yinxiang District. After the marriage, the couple was initially harmonious, but recently Lin Geng's behavior changed drastically. He neglected his business, frequented brothels, and paid no attention to his family, treating his wife like a thorn in his side. He also pawned all of Xiuling's dowry and ornaments. When Xiuling kindly advised him, she was beaten. This spring, she attempted suicide by drowning but was rescued by neighbors and survived. Zuquan then sent Xiuling back to her parents' home. However, Xiuling, due to her husband's immorality and repeated beatings, was constantly in tears and lamented her misfortune. She repeatedly attempted to hang herself to end her life, but her mother always detected it beforehand and persuaded her. Recently, Lin Geng pretended to repent and went to his in-laws' house to lure Xiuling back, intending to sell her. Xiuling found out and fled back to her parents' home to tell her father. Zuquan was furious when he heard that his son-in-law was so vicious and that it would be impossible to live together. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, he invited relatives and the matchmaker from both sides to Xu's house for a major negotiation. As a result, Lin Geng wrote an agreement, and both parties dissolved the marriage relationship and severed their marital ties.

Woman Accuses Husband of Bigamy and Abandonment; Verdict to be Announced

Zhang Yuan, a woman, sued her husband, Zhang Miaolin, in the local court for bigamy and abandonment, requesting a divorce. The court has held two hearings, but the defendant has failed to appear, preventing a final resolution. Yesterday morning, another hearing was held, and both the plaintiff and the defendant appeared as summoned. The plaintiff, Zhang Yuan, testified that she was 33 years old, a native of Sha, and currently resided at No. 98 Yuan Yu Lane, opposite the Sanxin Cotton Mill in Yangshupu. She said that the defendant beat her and committed bigamy with Zhang, which is why he drove her out. She returned to her mother's house on May 4th of this year. (Question) When did you marry? (Answer) We were married in October of the 11th year of the Republic [1922]. (Question) Did he injure you when he beat you? (Answer) Yes, I was injured. I reported it to the police station at the time, but they said it wasn't their concern. After Zhang entered the family, the defendant ordered me to move to the back building, which I refused to do, so he abused me. (Question) Why didn't you sue him for bigamy at the time? (Answer) I didn't understand. (Question) Why don't you sue him now that you know? (Answer) I am mindful of our marital relationship and took a step back, so I didn't file a lawsuit, etc. Next, Zhang Miaolin testified that he was 31 years old, a native of Nanhui, and ran the Zhang Guoji Red Gang Clothing Store at No. 6 Tianlin Lane, Tiantong'an. He said that the plaintiff was his legal wife. (Question) Why did you beat her? (Answer) I didn't beat her. (Question) Why did you marry Zhang again? (Answer) Zhang is her little sister; she is not a wife. (Question) If she is not a wife, why did you order the plaintiff to move to the back building? (Answer) I didn't move her. (Question) You are an artisan who already has a wife and still wants to take a concubine. Do you know that you are breaking the law now? (Answer) It was the plaintiff's suggestion. I treated the plaintiff very well. She was walking on the road with a shop worker on April 6th of this year, which I witnessed, etc. The judge asked the plaintiff, "You have been married for many years. Is it still possible to reconcile?" The plaintiff answered, "I must divorce him to protect my life." The judge then questioned the defendant, "Zhang was married in February of this year. How can she have a child who is about to have a full moon?" (Answer) We knew each other for a long time. The official said, "If Zhang does not leave, then the plaintiff cannot be with you." (Answer) Divorce is possible, but I spent 1,400 yuan to marry her, which should be returned." The official said, "How about an unconditional divorce with no returns?" The defendant said, "I don't want to." Then the arguments began, with lawyers for both sides debating each other. The defendant's lawyer claimed that the plaintiff had cohabitated with clothing craftsman Lu Xigen in a rented house on North Sichuan Road and that the landlord could prove it. Prosecutor Lei then came to the court to express his opinion. The judge then announced that the debate was over and that the verdict would be announced at 10:00 AM on the 15th of this month.

Teasing a Female Worker in a Vacant Lot

Two Months' Imprisonment Suspended

Husband Takes Her Back and Disciplines Her

Zhang Zhongwen, who resides at No. 97 Min Ti Ni Yin Road in the French Concession, hired lawyer Yao Zhaodi yesterday to represent him in the French court's criminal court, alleging that the plaintiff had married Wu as his wife more than ten years ago, and they had children. Young Woman Zhu Suzhen Accuses Kong Jingqing of Neglecting Support

The identity issue will be determined before further questioning.

Zhu Suzhen, a young woman from Kunshan who resides in Chengji Lane, North Zhejiang Road, recently accused her husband, Kong Jingqing, of neglecting her support. The case was heard in the Special District Local Court yesterday morning. The defendant did not appear. According to Zhu, she was a prostitute before the defendant became a customer. Later, because they were both happy, they talked about marriage. At the end of the 14th year [1925], she married him as a concubine. At the end of the 15th year [1926], the defendant took her to the Ping'an Small Hotel on Edward Road, claiming to take her back to his hometown in Ningbo, and left her in the hotel. The defendant never came back. At that time, she was four months pregnant. Later, because she had been waiting for a long time and did not see the defendant, she rented a place to live alone and has been living on borrowed money ever since. What she is asking for now is to order the defendant to pay her support money of 8,000 yuan, etc. The defendant's lawyer argued that the plaintiff was initially the defendant's concubine, but she has been separated from him for four years. The child she gave birth to cannot be recognized by the defendant. Because they have been separated for a long time and have nothing to do with each other, the defendant did not appear in court today, etc. The plaintiff's lawyer claimed that the defendant currently works for a foreign company and that his father-in-law is a compradore for the company. The defendant is deeply afraid that this matter will be known to his father-in-law, which is also a reason for the abandonment. In addition, the defendant once forced the plaintiff to borrow 10,000 yuan from her sister. Because the plaintiff's sister is married to a wealthy merchant, the plaintiff had no choice but to ask her sister for a loan, but she was refused. Seeing that the loan was unsuccessful, the defendant also denied the biological child. In fact, the child is indeed the defendant's and there is evidence to prove it. If the defendant were to appear in court today, he would probably be saddened by the plight of the plaintiff and her son, who are helpless, etc. Judge Yang instructed that the identity issue of the plaintiff should be determined before further interrogation.

Wang Mengnian Sentenced to Ten Years for Counterfeiting Currency

In addition to a fine of 1,000 yuan

Wang Mengnian, a native of Jiangbei, has been punished by the authorities twice before for counterfeiting currency. He did not repent and secretly set up a counterfeiting machine for auxiliary coins in a house at No. 455 Edward Road, disrupting the financial system. Han Peisheng, a detective of the exchange company, found out about it and secretly searched the house at 5:45 PM the other day, confiscating 971 counterfeit double dimes, 34 single dimes, and more than 20 battery molds. Yesterday, he was sent to the Special District Local Court for investigation. Wang confessed that it was done by two Xu who are on the run. Judge Wu verified the confession and sentenced Wang Mengnian to ten years of imprisonment and a fine of 1,000 yuan. If he is unable to pay, he will be imprisoned for an additional year. The counterfeit coins were confiscated.

Child's Body Drowned Due to Careless Swimming

At 12:10 PM yesterday, the body of a boy was found in the Suzhou River near the Wusong Wharf. He was about twelve or thirteen years old and had no clothes on. It is likely that he fell into the river due to careless swimming and drowned. The Chinese police of the No. 14 Water Patrol Station recovered the body and sent it to the Salvation Bureau for collection.

Xu Gengshou Drowned in the River

Xu Gengshou, a native of Changshu, earned a living by steering wharf boats. Yesterday afternoon around 3:00 PM, Xu was contracted to load 200 bags of white rice from Dingtai Company in Pudong and transport them to the Santai Wharf in Puxi for transshipment to Taizhou native Liu Zhenfu's Jiangbei boat for transport to other ports. Unexpectedly, after arriving at the wharf, Xu was about to transfer the rice bags to Liu's boat. Because of the hot weather, Liu refused to start the transshipment and agreed to postpone it until evening. Xu refused because he did not have time, which led to an argument between the two that escalated into a major conflict. As a result, Xu lost his balance while standing on the rice bags, slipped, and fell into the river. By the time they managed to rescue him onto the boat, Xu was already dead. Xu's wife, Lu, arrived after hearing the news and took Liu Zhenfu to the Water Patrol Team of the Public Security Bureau to demand punishment. After questioning by Team Leader Xu during the preliminary hearing, Liu confessed that he was 34 years old and that the deceased Xu Gengshou was flirting with his sister on the boat at the time. When he saw it, he scolded him. Xu was ashamed and angry and cursed back, jumping around between the rice bags and accidentally slipping into the river. He did not beat him, etc. The team leader, considering that the case involved a human life and was important, ordered that the original complaint be prepared and that the parties be transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for interrogation.

Male Corpse Run Over by a Car Found at the Huacheng Road Intersection

At around 11:00 AM yesterday morning, a pedestrian run over by a vehicle was found at the intersection of Huacheng Road, Yangshupu. The victim was about 30 years old, looked like a worker, and was wearing a white cloth shirt, blue cloth pants, bare feet, and straw sandals. His skull was broken and covered in blood, a tragic sight. Street police No. 2704 arrived and transported the body to Tongren Hospital and then to the coroner's office for examination.

Teahouse Worker Killed After Being Hit By Car

Zheng Qingfang, 39 years old, a native of Ningbo who worked as a teahouse worker at the Hongkou Grand Hotel on North Sichuan Road, was walking near Dongyouheng Road at 7:00 AM yesterday when a No. 5397 cargo truck from the Tailong Flour Company suddenly drove by. Zheng tried to avoid it but was knocked to the ground, his left leg crushed. The scene was too gruesome to bear. Police No. 2570 checked and found a hired car to send him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, the wound was too large, and he bled excessively. He died at 2:30 PM.

Two Boats Collide, Child Falls into the Water

The Father Was Saddened

Xun Laosi, a native of Yancheng, was engaged in boating. At that time, Zhao Xinli, a native of Qingpu, was driving a boat and accidentally collided with Xun Laosi's boat. Public Security Bureau Raises Positions of Secretaries, etc. in Various District Offices

The district offices of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau handle prohibited cases on a daily basis. Each district office has one or two secretaries and scribes who specialize in writing reports and preparing documents, which are carried out under the supervision of the district chiefs. Director Yuan believes that the territory under the jurisdiction of each district office is vast, and the population is increasing daily. All daily prohibited cases are extremely complicated. It is impossible for anyone with mediocre talent and knowledge to handle the work of the secretaries and scribes in each district office. He now plans to carefully screen and raise the positions, renaming the position of secretary to document officer and the position of scribe to clerk. A notice has now been issued to the captains of the various district offices to conduct strict assessments and submit them for review.

Minutes of the Executive Committee of the Lǐ-ism Society

The Shanghai Lǐ-ism United Association held an executive committee meeting yesterday. Chairman Zhang Yichen presided over the meeting. After reporting on the agenda, the following matters were discussed: (1) The case of Ye Mingbai and others from the Lǐ-ism branch in Liu'an, Anhui, requesting the establishment of a Lǐ-ism branch association was resolved. It was decided that Lǐ-ism does not have branch associations, and it should be changed to the Lǐ-ism XX Hall for Abstaining from Alcohol and Tobacco. (2) Hu Huiren reported on the temporary maintenance of the Jishantang Public Hall in Haimen. It was decided to reply by letter and proceed with the change. (3) The Deyuantang Public Hall in Fengyang, Anhui, proposed to establish a Lǐ-ism United Association. It was decided that there are only a few public halls in that area, so they can be directly affiliated with the association without establishing another one. (4) The Yushantang Public Hall in Ning'an, Jilin, sent a letter requesting membership. It was decided to ask them to correct the name first and not use the name Lǐshàn. (5) The Fushantang Public Hall in Pei County, Jiangsu, inquired about the reorganization situation and regulations. It was decided to reply by letter, instructing all public halls in the county to uniformly change to Lǐ-ism XX Hall for Abstaining from Alcohol and Tobacco. (6) The Pushantang Public Hall in Changshu reported that the Renshantang Public Hall violated the rules of Lǐ-ism. It was decided that the public hall was falsely using the name of Lǐ-ism, and the Changshu County Government should be requested to strictly ban it by letter. (7) The Shantang Public Hall in Jingjiang, Jiangsu, sent a letter requesting membership and protection. It was decided to reply by letter. (8) Ma Changfu and others from the Yizheng Wenshantang Public Hall requested the issuance of a seal. It was decided to reply by letter. (9) The local Pushantang Public Hall reported that it was refused rent by the landlord and illegally evicted, requesting assistance. It was decided to publicly recommend the chairman to negotiate seriously with the landlord. (10) The sixth election case of the association was resolved. It was decided to inform the Lǐ-ism Public Halls to send the resumes of the representatives attending this session to the association within five days. Other cases were omitted.

Book and Newspaper Introductions

A Bird's-Eye View of New Works by European Writers: Two Brothers (Manru)

A novel by the French writer Prévost

Maurois recently said, "Prophecy is a dangerous thing, but I will still make a prediction. I will tell you the names of three writers who are not yet thirty years old. If my guess is correct, these three people will occupy very important positions in French literature in the future. These three people are André Chanson, André Malraux, and Jean Prévost." Now we want to talk about the last one, Prévost, because he recently published a novel (Les Frères Bouquinquant).

Prévost is a short, fat man with yellow hair and blue eyes. His forehead is lined, and his face is like a pirate. He is a very enthusiastic athlete and a good boxer. He studied at the École Normale Supérieure, which is both beneficial and dangerous for a writer. It is beneficial because it can provide its students with a very thorough education. It is dangerous because it can make its students unable to get rid of the pedantic habit of quoting scriptures and chewing words for life.

Fortunately, Prévost himself has an amazing energy and a superb taste. He overcame all the elements that could damage his talent, thus becoming a rising talent in the French literary world. He has now written two books, both of which are extraordinary works. The first one is Dix-huitième Année, which very faithfully and sincerely depicts the life of a French young student holding progressive ideas right after the European War. This is a confession and an autobiography. The second one, which was just published, is Les Frères Bouquinquant, a novel about the life of the masses with many advantages.

The plot is very ordinary. The plot can almost be found in the archives of the police station. Remember (André Gide) loved to use this kind of plot. The story is about a young mechanic who became his sister-in-law's lover on a Seine barge. Later, he killed his brother because his brother beat his sister-in-law. When the matter was discovered, the woman admitted that she had committed the murder. In this way, she saved her lover, and her lover had no choice but to accept her sacrifice. The plot is roughly like this, but the story itself is not important. What is important is the author's novel approach and special style of depicting workers. Most writers write about the lives of workers by observing from the outside, without understanding the people themselves, so they often fail to be accurate. For example, Zola's characters, although epic in their grandeur, are not realistic. Prévost is different. His book is full of reality. He writes out the complexity of their character. He makes us understand that the moral standards of the masses are often different from those of the bourgeoisie, but their desires are the same. This novel can be said to have exhausted the psychology of the French people.

Prévost has great ambitions for this novel. His wish is to write this novel like Hugo's "Les Misérables." This is naturally an exaggeration, but the ambition of this young writer can be seen from this.

Loti Sheya (Manru)

A novel by the French writer Jolo

In the current literary world of Paris, few people are as famous as Edmond Jaloux. First, he is a critic of Les Nouvelles Littéraires with a very good reputation. He has introduced many foreign literary works to French readers, and these works have had a very good influence. Second, he has always been willing to help young writers, so his interpersonal relationships are very good. Third, he is the first Frenchman to introduce new German literature and has a very good relationship with Hofmannsthal and others.

But Jolo is not just a critic, he is also a novelist, especially a truly talented person. His knowledge, wisdom, and sensitive conversations are very tempting. People who meet him for the first time see his calm face and slow, elegant voice and always think he is a quiet and pragmatic person. But after a while, they will find that he is a person full of mysterious emotions and poetic interests. Jolo's books are like his conversations. In his books and in his conversations, the most lovely thing is the feeling that there is a more beautiful world in front of you, and this more beautiful world is entirely composed of the memories of the books he has read, which is the synthesis of the literary fantasy world.

His book "Loetitia" is written with this kind of poetry. It tells the story of the girl Loetitia. Loetitia fell in love with a great German poet, Walter Graul. However, she does not know him and has never met him. Graul's personality is very similar to two great poets. The quality of his poems is like Rilke, and his need for a woman is like Shelley. Every woman, before he lives with her, he regards as a celestial bodhisattva. But once he lives with her and discovers that she is just an ordinary person, he is very dissatisfied and immediately destroys his own idol. Loetitia, like other women, was destroyed in this way.

These few short sentences cannot express the magic of this novel. Jolo wrote this novel as if Allan Poe was writing "The Fall of the House of Usher," shrouding the failure history of this beautiful love in a mysterious and vague atmosphere, making readers involuntarily feel depressed and sad.

The Wilderness Society Establishes a Publishing Department

The Shanghai Wilderness Society at 34 Ferren Road has been established for one year. The sales of published books and series are extremely popular, and especially the Wilderness News published every week is most popular among the industrial, commercial, and academic circles. Literary news has made publishers and writers compete to spread the word. Recently, due to the printing of various creative works, the Wilderness News will publish Volume 3, Issue 1. The original address of the society is not enough, so the publishing department has been expanded and moved to B1723, Jiangyuan Lane, Xinzha Road, inside the Paili Printing Company. Office hours are from 1:00 PM to 6:00 PM every day. If you want to join the society, subscribe to the newspaper, or inquire about the publishing department, please contact the office nearby. The original address of the society will still maintain normal office hours from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM and from 7:00 PM to 10:00 PM. When the Wilderness News publishes Volume 3, Issue 1, it will solicit members for the second time.

Manuscript Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Introductions

(1) The text should be limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all political, economic, legal, scientific, educational, etc. books and newspapers are included in the introduction. However, boring books will not be introduced.

(2) Texts on the textual research or research of ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(3) Pictures and photos are limited to those related to the text.

(4) Each text should not exceed 3,000 characters.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(6) Do not write the manuscript horizontally and do not write in a sloppy manner. Western text should be omitted where possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink to draw the attached pictures in the manuscript, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black drawing.

(8) Please indicate that the manuscript is to be received by the Book and Newspaper Introduction Department.

(9) Manuscripts will not be returned regardless of whether they are published or not. If you need to return them, you should declare it in advance and attach sufficient postage stamps.

(10) Remuneration: The remuneration for texts is divided into three types: four yuan, three yuan, and two yuan per thousand characters. The same applies to each picture and photo. If there are special manuscripts, the remuneration will be calculated separately.

Youth Corner

The Dramatic Movement That Youth Should Strive For (Ji Ping)

The dramatic movement seems to have recently attracted social attention. Generally, those engaged in this movement are eagerly hoping for its success. This naturally provides them with some comfort. However, what exactly is its content in reality? What kind of impression does it give us? This cannot but make us feel a huge crisis.

There are probably dozens of theater groups in Shanghai, including small-scale organizations in various schools. In the past few months, we have seen the two public performances of the Art Theater Society, the "Dog's Dance" of the Xin You Theater Society, the "Merchant of Venice" of the Drama Association, and the recent "Carmen" and Fudan Society's "Cyrano." In the process of these performances, we can see that there has been considerable attention paid to both the theater and the actual performance. However, "the most important scripts" make people shake their heads in disappointment. Except for the Art Society and the Drama Association's "All Quiet on the Western Front" and "Ah Zhen," which contain sufficient propaganda meaning and serve as political tools, most of the rest can be said to be biased towards romantic love affairs, mainly for the meaning of enjoyment. These are indeed constrained by the current society, that is, the general preference of the current society is such, and in order to cater to the psychology, it has to be so. However, as a result, we feel that apart from sexual hints to young people, there is nothing else. Is this nothing else the main purpose of our dramatic movement?

Drama is a comprehensive art. It is an art that directly expresses human life with sound, color, and moving three-dimensionality, that is, with time and space. Based on the synthesis of all senses, it makes people feel. Its artistic expression style is the most complex and closest to the style of human life. Therefore, it is required by the majority of people and has a profound and broad intrusive special power into the majority of people. In ancient societies, the occurrence of drama was very early. It is a product of the nation and a representation of national culture. Especially in religious countries, it has become a ceremony to respect the gods. However, in the autocratic feudal society, it has mostly become a tool for the emperors to anesthetize the majority of people, and the content of the drama is only "going to the capital to seek fame" and "eliminating evil and evil." This kind of old drama is still preserved in the countryside and cities, and the past emotions and emotions that have been infected are still very rich. In such a situation in the drama world, it is necessary for us to rise up to overcome this kind of toxic and build a new drama. This necessity has produced the dramatic movement. Since the dramatic movement has become a movement, it is naturally not just a natural occurrence, but a purposeful and conscious effort. But this effort has been going on for quite a period of time. What are its results? This cannot but disappoint us, because not only has the old toxic not been overcome, but the so-called new construction is just the same toxic thing. As mentioned above, the central content of this movement at present, apart from being used as some kind of propaganda, is some romantic things. The result of this kind of thing can only weaken the heroic ambition of young people and create a decadent attitude, and this tendency is now flourishing. Isn't this still a huge crisis?

This crisis is not only about the dramatic movement itself, but also about the future of the nation. Therefore, we must overcome it, and how is this overcoming done?

First, establish a central consciousness. We feel that in the past, the drama movement has seemed to have done a considerable amount of effort to abandon the old drama, but for the new construction, it only knows to pursue innovation blindly, and there is no central consciousness to choose. As a result, it only sells some foreign works to cater to the psychology of low-level tastes, and it is fragmented and cannot give people upward hints, let alone what national culture is. Therefore, in order to require this movement to truly shoulder the great mission in practice, it can only be carried out systematically by establishing a central consciousness as its foundation, generate real power in the masses, and become the highest expression of national culture.

Secondly, the construction of nationalism and the establishment of a central consciousness have become the urgent needs of the current dramatic movement. There is no doubt about this in theory. But what is it that can truly serve as a central consciousness? This can naturally only be determined in the objective facts of the society. We know that drama is originally a product of the nation. Naturally, its highest value can only be estimated from the point of view of promoting the national spirit and upholding national interests. In other words, its greatest task is to promote the evolution of the nation. What is the Chinese nation like now? Undoubtedly, it is trapped in the position of a semi-colonial country that cannot be independent, and the legacy of past feudal consciousness and the current depression are enough to destroy the power of the nation and tend to a more difficult situation. Therefore, the central consciousness of our dramatic movement today must be the construction of nationalism. Starting from this, we must eliminate all things that are coy, obscene, decadent, and harmful to the nation, and awaken the national consciousness, inspire the national vigor, beautify the national life, and concentrate the national strength to fight for the nation in unity. Only in this way can the meaning of the drama itself be unfolded, and only in this way can the mission of this movement be completed.

Furthermore, organize a powerful drama troupe. The crisis and the method of overcoming the general dramatic movement have been theoretically indicated above, but the main thing is still the significance of practice. What is the significance of practice? That can only be the organization of a powerful drama troupe to work hard for this proposition. We know that there are indeed many drama troupes in Shanghai now.

But they all only have negative power and are the root cause of this movement. Therefore, the organization of this powerful drama troupe is necessary, and it must be to overcome the unsound theories and actions of other drama troupes and stand in a leading position as the center of a new movement.

In short, with the progress of history, the past dramatic movement has gradually lost all its significance and has fallen into a huge crisis. Now is the time to break through this crisis and open up a new situation. And this new situation, based on the needs of objective society and accompanying the recent trend of the literary and artistic movement, is inevitably nationalistic. And those who bear this responsibility are inevitably promising young people. Because the talents of drama are multi-faceted, it needs the power of vitality and enthusiasm, sincerity and evolution...and this power is only possessed by young people. At the same time, the liberation of the Chinese nation at present is entrusted to the youth, and the work of the liberation movement is especially to awaken the national consciousness. Drama is the most infectious, so the dramatic movement is an important and powerful part of the whole process of the liberation movement. Only when young people are combined with the purposeful nature of this movement can they be liberated from the current crisis and stand firmly on the stand of nationalism to open up a bloody path, practice the significance of the dramatic movement, and complete the mission that young people should have.
